### Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction UI invariants

These rows are Phase 3.8 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an Operator Stream Interaction UI surface that extends the existing Operator TUI parser, session, snapshot, and render paths with a finite typed route over the accepted Phase 3.7 Text Stream Ingress substrate. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, social/language harnesses, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls (the explicit Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle owns the model-backed seam), real host execution, text-stream serialization or weaving into traces or scenarios, an aggregate "quality" / "intelligence" / "social-success" score, automatic promotion, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The Phase 3.8 stream surface appends bounded operator text to session-local `TextStreamHistory`, exposes read-only summary and candidate views over the Phase 3.7 substrate, and queues exactly one explicit `StreamPromotionCandidate` per `/stream-promote` call through the existing `OperatorEventQueue` surface; `/step` remains the only route that calls `tick()`. The stream surface produces no parse trees, no language meaning, no truth claims, no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, no agency witnesses, no second classification paths, and no aggregate quality scores.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-UISTRM-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command parser is finite and typed. | `LocalCommandLine.parse(line)` accepts exactly `/stream`, `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, and `/stream-promote` in addition to the existing approved verbs; each verb maps to a fixed `OperatorCommand` and a frozen `Command` payload; lines beginning with any other token, missing required arguments, or carrying non-printable / over-bound text return a `LocalCommandError` with bounded printable text without reaching `OperatorSession.event_queue` or `OperatorSession` stream state. | `brain/ui/command_line.py` | `stream_command_parser.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command payloads are bounded and constructor-checked. | `/stream` text is non-empty bounded printable raw text compatible with `TextStreamChunk` (length at most `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN`); `/stream-promote` `candidate_id` is bounded printable text (length at most `STREAM_PROMOTION_MAX`); stream command payload records are frozen and carry no callable, file handle, socket, LLM client, subprocess handle, or path object; payload construction with empty, non-printable, over-length, or `COGITO_ID`-equal values raises `ValueError` or returns `LocalCommandError` without partially mutating session state. | `brain/ui/command_line.py` | `stream_command_parser.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream` appends to session-local `TextStreamHistory` only. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.STREAM_APPEND` constructs one `TextStreamChunk` with `TextStreamSource.OPERATOR` via the accepted Phase 3.7 constructor and returns updated session-local stream state with the new chunk appended through `TextStreamHistory.append`; before and after dispatch, `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `latest_tick`, `tick_counter`, `OutputHistory`, `WorldletHistory`, `ProtoBasicHistory`, `ExpressionHistory`, `OperatorTranscript`, and `OperatorSession.event_queue` identities and serializations are unchanged. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_session_append.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream-summary` is read-only. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.INSPECT_STREAM_SUMMARY` selects a stream-summary view on `OperatorSession` and may build immutable summary snapshots over local `TextStreamHistory` and exact `int` / `Fraction` aggregate counts; before and after dispatch, local stream history identity / length / chunks, `StreamPromotionCandidate` records, `BrainState`, source histories, `OperatorSession.event_queue`, `latest_tick`, and `tick_counter` are unchanged; the dispatch never calls `tick()`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_summary_candidates.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream-candidates` is read-only. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.INSPECT_STREAM_CANDIDATES` selects a stream-candidate view on `OperatorSession` and may build immutable candidate snapshots from `SegmentCandidate`, `StreamPattern`, and `StreamPromotionCandidate` records derived from local stream history; before and after dispatch, local stream history, candidate records, `BrainState`, source histories, `OperatorSession.event_queue`, `latest_tick`, and `tick_counter` are unchanged; the dispatch never calls `tick()`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_summary_candidates.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/stream-promote` queues exactly one validated candidate and does not tick. | Dispatching `OperatorCommand.STREAM_PROMOTE` resolves exactly one explicit `StreamPromotionCandidate` by `candidate_id`, converts it to one `QueuePerceptPayload` through the same constructor-bounded path used by `/queue` (`PerceptEvent`-constructor checked, non-reserved `target_content_id`, bounded printable text, no callable / resource / client fields), and enqueues it through `OperatorEventQueue.enqueue`; the dispatch does not call `tick()`, does not call `dequeue`, does not append to private queue storage directly, does not mutate `BrainState`, `latest_tick`, or `tick_counter`, and leaves `OperatorSession.event_queue` length increased by exactly one on success. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_promotion_queue.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | `/step` remains the only stream interaction path that calls `tick()`. | Across `/stream`, `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, and `/stream-promote` dispatches, `OperatorSession.tick_counter`, `OperatorSession.latest_tick`, and the underlying `BrainState` identity are unchanged; only `OperatorCommand.STEP_TICK` reaches the existing `_dispatch_step` route that invokes the public `tick()` entrypoint with the queued events and current `BrainState`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_tick_boundary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command failure paths are local UI status/error only. | For malformed `/stream` input, over-bound `/stream` text, non-printable text, unknown `/stream-promote` `candidate_id`, candidate-to-payload constructor rejection, `PerceptEvent` validation failure, and a full `OperatorEventQueue`, the router records the failure as bounded local UI status/error text on `OperatorSession` and leaves `BrainState`, `ScalarProfile`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `latest_tick`, `tick_counter`, source histories, `OperatorTranscript`, and `OperatorSession.event_queue` length unchanged; only successful `/stream-promote` increases `OperatorSession.event_queue` length by exactly one. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_failure_isolation.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream snapshots and render output are deterministic and read-only. | For equal stream interaction state and equal view-model inputs, stream-summary and stream-candidate snapshots and rendered rows are equal across repeated calls; snapshot construction and rendering mutate no `TextStreamHistory`, no `StreamPromotionCandidate` record, no `BrainState`, no source history, no `OperatorSession.event_queue`, no trace event, no scenario file, and no catalog file; rendering performs no curses call from pure snapshot/render paths and no file or network I/O. | `brain/ui/snapshot.py` + `brain/ui/render.py` | `stream_snapshot_render.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream interaction introduces no language / truth / social / agency / Mode B / model-backed behavior. | A static AST audit over the Phase 3.8 stream additions in `brain/ui/commands.py`, `brain/ui/command_line.py`, `brain/ui/session.py`, `brain/ui/snapshot.py`, `brain/ui/render.py`, and `brain/ui/fixtures/stream_*` rejects any parser / grammar / semantic / dialogue surface, any truth flag / `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` / readability score / agency witness / Mode B planner field, any second classification path, any real LLM call site, and any direct `tick()` call outside the existing `_dispatch_step` route; stream snapshots and views expose only structural raw text counts, segments, recurrence patterns, and explicit promotion candidates. | `brain/ui/` | `stream_static_audit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-UISTRM-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream session state is resource-free and local. | The session-owned stream interaction state (whether attached to `OperatorSession` directly or carried by a `StreamInteractionState` field) holds only `TextStreamHistory`, bounded immutable `StreamPromotionCandidate` tuples, and bounded printable identifiers; it holds no real LLM client, no subprocess handle, no file descriptor, no network socket, no path object intended for save/export, no shell command for execution, no callback, and no mutable reference into source histories. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `stream_session_resource_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UISTRM-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream UI records are immutable display / payload values. | Stream command payload records, stream interaction state records, stream-summary snapshots, and stream-candidate snapshots are frozen dataclasses or equivalent immutable records; fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded primitives, strings for exact `Fraction` display values, or frozen Phase 3.7 text-stream records; no mutable kernel container is stored on these records. | `brain/ui/snapshot.py` | `stream_snapshot_render.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UISTRM-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream UI static audit rejects forbidden side effects. | A static AST audit over the Phase 3.8 stream additions in `brain/ui/commands.py`, `brain/ui/command_line.py`, `brain/ui/session.py`, `brain/ui/snapshot.py`, `brain/ui/render.py`, and `brain/ui/fixtures/stream_*` rejects `os.system`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `pathlib` write paths, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `brain.llm`, `brain.tlica` mutation surfaces, `curses` from pure parser / snapshot / render paths, real LLM call sites, and any `tick()` call outside the existing `_dispatch_step` dispatch. | `brain/ui/` | `stream_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UISTRM-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream UI constants preserve Phase 3.7 bounds. | `STREAM_TEXT_MAX_LEN == 1024`, `STREAM_PROVENANCE_MAX_LEN == 64`, `STREAM_PROMOTION_MAX == 64`, `LOCAL_CMD_MAX_ERROR_LEN == 240`, and `MAX_STATUS_TEXT_LEN == 240`; the Phase 3.8 stream UI imports these from their owning modules where possible, and any copied value has explicit fixture parity against the owning module constants. | `brain/ui/` | `stream_constant_parity.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UISTRM-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream command constructors are pure and register no callbacks. | A static AST audit over the Phase 3.8 stream additions in `brain/ui/commands.py`, `brain/ui/command_line.py`, `brain/ui/session.py`, `brain/ui/snapshot.py`, `brain/ui/render.py`, and `brain/ui/fixtures/stream_*` rejects module-level side effects, registry mutations, callback registrations, `atexit` handlers, decorator-installed hooks, source-history mutator calls, and event-queue mutations outside the explicit `/stream-promote` dispatch path. | `brain/ui/` | `stream_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-UISTRM-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Scripted stream interaction walk is inspectable. | A deterministic scripted operator session (`/stream hello world`, `/stream hello world`, `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, `/stream-promote <candidate_id>`, `/step`, `/tick`) over an injected deterministic tick client records parser results, dispatched `OperatorSession` routes, stream history counts, candidate queueing through `OperatorEventQueue.enqueue`, `TickRecord` production after `/step` only, and absence of kernel-boundary leaks; the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. The walk is documented in `docs/campaigns/archive/PHASE3_8_OPERATOR_STREAM_INTERACTION_AUDIT.md`. | `brain/ui/session.py` | (none) | OBSERVED |
| I-UISTRM-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8 Operator Stream Interaction) | Stream UI save / export path is NOT-EXERCISED. | No Phase 3.8 Operator TUI stream save, export, serialization, trace weaving, scenario weaving, or write-to-disk path exists in this campaign; any future write path requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, dedicated catalog rows that constrain the path, fixtures that exercise the path under bounded conditions, and a stop condition for failure modes; this row exists so a future campaign cannot quietly add filesystem writes from stream UI surfaces without registering coverage. | `brain/ui/` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |

### Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle UI invariants

These rows are Phase 3.8b engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit operator-facing LLM Runtime Toggle that adds one CLI surface (`--llm-mode <mode>`) plus a small typed helper module (`brain/ui/llm_runtime.py`) on top of the existing `LLMClient` protocol and the existing `tick(..., client, ...)` seam. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize a non-offline default, automatic credential / tool detection without opt-in, an environment read inside `build_llm_client_from_config`, a new `LLMClient` implementation beyond the four shipped backends, a second classification path alongside the existing `tick()` route, model-backed scoring of stream evidence, model output reaching traces / scenarios / source histories, a new `tick()` argument signature, mid-session mode flips, a curses key binding for mode selection, an implicit cache enable, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The toggle surfaces a finite closed `LlmRuntimeMode` (`OFFLINE`, `MOCK`, `ANTHROPIC_API`, `CLAUDE_CLI`); a frozen / slots-bearing `LlmRuntimeConfig`; a `parse_llm_runtime_args(argv, env)` parser that resolves `api_key` from CLI then `BRAIN_ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` then `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (supplied env only); a `build_llm_client_from_config(config)` factory that never reads `os.environ`, raises `LlmRuntimeError` locally before launch when the explicit config is insufficient, and returns an `LLMClient`-compatible client (or a `CachedClient` wrapping the backend when caching is opt-in for `ANTHROPIC_API` / `CLAUDE_CLI`); and the entrypoint plumbing that passes the resolved client into `run_curses(session, client=..., ...)` so the selected client enters the kernel through the existing `tick()` seam. Default behavior remains offline: every existing REQUIRED and STRUCTURAL fixture passes with no `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, no `BRAIN_ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, and no `claude` executable on PATH. The optional real model-backed smoke walk is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner; the LLM runtime save / export path is NOT-EXERCISED. The toggle introduces no parse trees, no language meaning, no truth claims, no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, no agency witnesses, no aggregate quality scores, no second classification path, and no automatic promotion.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |

| I-LLMTOG-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle) | Default `LlmRuntimeConfig()` builds `OfflineStandInClient`. | `LlmRuntimeConfig()` with no arguments produces a record whose `mode` is `LlmRuntimeMode.OFFLINE` and whose `enable_cache` is `False`; `build_llm_client_from_config(LlmRuntimeConfig())` returns an instance of `OfflineStandInClient` and does not consult `os.environ`. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_default_offline.py` | REQUIRED |

With `enable_cache=True` and `ANTHROPIC_API` / `CLAUDE_CLI`, the returned client is a `CachedClient` wrapping the expected backend, and the cache directory is the `brain/.llm_cache` default. | `brain/ui/llm_runtime.py` | `llm_runtime_cache_gated.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store invariants

These rows are Phase 3.9 engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit, typed, transactional, schema-versioned SQLite-backed persistent session store at `brain/ui/persistence.py` over the existing `BrainState` + `OperatorSession` surface. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize multi-profile / multi-user persistence, network-backed persistence, migrations between schema versions in v1, persistence of LLM client / cache / runtime mode, persistence of operator transcripts beyond bounded session-local state, persistence of curses configuration / terminal state, raw-text-to-`COGITO_ID` mappings, raw-text-to-`BrainState` direct writes, changes to `tick()` semantics, new typed operator commands outside `/save-session` and `/load-session`, save / export paths outside the configured session DB, autosave from `/step`, `/stream`, `/stream-promote`, or any other tick-adjacent dispatch path, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The store records, on `/save-session`, the operator-visible kernel state (`ScalarProfile` values, `MSI` contents and threshold, `PtCns` `eval_map`, `ContentRegistry` texts) plus the Phase 3.7 / 3.8 session-local stream state (`tick_counter`, `stream_chunk_serial`, `TextStreamHistory` chunks, and `StreamPromotionCandidate` records when present) into a finite closed v1 schema with `num INTEGER + den INTEGER` `Fraction` columns and no `REAL` kernel-numeric column. On `/load-session` it re-reads the typed rows in `sqlite3` uri `mode=ro`, builds `Persistent*Snapshot` records, reconstructs the candidate `OperatorSession` through the existing public builders (`make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns`, `ContentRegistry(...)`, `BrainState(profile=, msi=, ptcns=, registry=)`, `make_text_stream_chunk`, `TextStreamHistory(chunks=...)`, `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, `OperatorSession(state=, ...)`), runs invariant assertions, and returns the candidate session only if every step succeeds. Failed saves roll back the `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` / `COMMIT` transaction and never mutate the live `OperatorSession`. Failed loads (missing DB, wrong file type, missing meta rows, unknown `schema_version`, `FOREIGN KEY` violations, malformed `Fraction` pairs, over-bound text, constructor / invariant rejection) raise `PersistenceError` and never replace the live session. `COGITO_ID` is reserved on load: a `profile_values` row at a non-canonical `COGITO_ID` value, a missing `msi_contents` `COGITO_ID` row, or a `ptcns_eval` row mapping `COGITO_ID` to a non-`PRESERVE` evaluation raises `PersistenceError`. `OperatorSession` remains resource-free with an optional `SessionStoreConfig` field; no `sqlite3.Connection` lives on `OperatorSession`. The persistence module imports only the documented seam set (stdlib `sqlite3`, `pathlib`, `datetime`, `fractions`, `dataclasses`, `typing` + `brain.io_types`, `brain.tick.BrainState` as a typed record, `brain.tlica.builders`, `brain.tlica.profile`, `brain.tlica.msi`, `brain.tlica.ptcns`, `brain.development.text_stream`, `brain.ui.session`, `brain.ui.commands`); it does not import `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, the `tick` callable from `brain.tick`, or anything that enables execution of persisted bytes (`eval`, `exec`, `compile`, `importlib.import_module`, `__import__`); module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring); no `@atexit` / signal / threading / asyncio autosave hook is registered. A cold-start continuity dry run is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. An autosave path is NOT-EXERCISED, structurally enforced by `persistence_static_audit.py` rejecting tick-adjacent and ambient-trigger autosave hooks; any future autosave requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, a dedicated catalog row, bounded fixtures, and a new stop condition.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-PERSIST-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | SQLite schema is finite and closed. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` defines exactly the v1 tables (`meta`, `content_registry`, `profile_values`, `msi_contents`, `msi_threshold`, `ptcns_eval`, `session_state`, `stream_chunks`, `stream_candidates`) with the documented columns, NOT NULL constraints, PRIMARY KEY / UNIQUE / FOREIGN KEY structure, and CHECK constraints (`rho_den > 0`, `den > 0`, `msi_threshold.id = 1`); no additional kernel-state table exists in v1. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_schema.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Unknown `schema_version` is rejected on load. | `load_session(config)` reads the `meta.schema_version` row, coerces to `int`, and raises `PersistenceError` with a bounded printable message when the value is not in `SUPPORTED_SCHEMA_VERSIONS`; the live `OperatorSession` is unchanged. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_failed_load.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | `fractions.Fraction` values persist exactly as integer pairs. | `save_session(...)` writes every `ScalarProfile` value and the `MSI` threshold as `(num INTEGER, den INTEGER)` rows; `load_session(...)` reconstructs them as `Fraction(num, den)` and the resulting `Fraction` values are byte-for-byte equal to the originals under `Fraction.__eq__`; no `float()` / `Decimal` / `REAL` column appears in any kernel-numeric path. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_save_roundtrip.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | `COGITO_ID` cannot be overwritten by persisted data. | A `profile_values` row with `content_id = COGITO_ID` and `rho != 1`, a missing `msi_contents` `COGITO_ID` row, or a `ptcns_eval` row mapping `COGITO_ID` to a non-`PRESERVE` evaluation raises `PersistenceError` on load; the live `OperatorSession` is unchanged; save of a session with `COGITO_ID` at value `1` round-trips exactly. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_cogito_protected.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Load reconstructs kernel state through public builders / constructors only. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` builds the candidate `OperatorSession` by calling `make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns`, `ContentRegistry(texts=MappingProxyType(...))`, `BrainState(profile=, msi=, ptcns=, registry=)`, `make_text_stream_chunk`, `TextStreamHistory(chunks=...)`, `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, and `OperatorSession(state=, ...)`; an AST audit confirms no attribute / private-field assignment on any kernel record, no `object.__setattr__` on frozen records, no `pickle.loads` / `shelve.open` / `marshal.loads`, and no `json.loads`-as-dict-direct-into-constructor on authoritative kernel state. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_load_constructor_only.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Load runs invariant assertions before returning. | After assembling the candidate state, `load_session(...)` invokes the existing invariant-assertion entrypoint (`assert_state_invariants` or its current equivalent) on the candidate `BrainState`; if the assertion raises, `load_session` raises `PersistenceError` and returns no candidate session. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_load_invariants.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Failed save preserves the live session. | If any `sqlite3.IntegrityError` / `OperationalError` / `DatabaseError` or constructor error is raised mid-save, the transaction rolls back and the live `OperatorSession` is unchanged; a subsequent successful save into the same DB produces a clean v1-shaped snapshot indistinguishable from one made without the injected failure. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_failed_save.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Failed load preserves the live session. | Missing DB, wrong file type, missing meta rows, unknown `schema_version`, `FOREIGN KEY` violations, malformed `Fraction` pairs, over-bound text, and constructor / invariant rejection all surface as `PersistenceError`; in each case the live `OperatorSession` is unchanged and the on-disk DB file is unchanged (load runs in sqlite3 uri `mode=ro`). | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_failed_load.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | `/save-session` and `/load-session` are bounded and local, and do not call `tick()`. | `LocalCommandLine.parse` accepts `/save-session` and `/load-session` as closed verbs and rejects trailing arguments; `_dispatch_save_session` and `_dispatch_load_session` on `OperatorSession` call `save_session` / `load_session`, surface bounded printable status / error text on the session, and never invoke `tick()`; both dispatchers fail closed on a missing `session_store_config`, leaving live state untouched. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_commands.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PERSIST-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Save transaction is atomic. | `save_session(...)` uses `sqlite3.connect(...)` with `isolation_level=None` and an explicit `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` / `COMMIT` pair; a mid-save failure triggers `ROLLBACK` and leaves no orphaned rows from the failed attempt; the next successful save into the same DB produces a snapshot indistinguishable from one made without the injected failure. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_atomic_save.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PERSIST-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | `OperatorSession` is resource-free with `SessionStoreConfig`. | `OperatorSession` may carry an `Optional[SessionStoreConfig]`; `_ALLOWED_SESSION_ATTRS` adds `"session_store_config"`; `SessionStoreConfig`'s fields are bounded (`pathlib.Path`, `int`, `str`); no `OperatorSession` or `SessionStoreConfig` field contains an `sqlite3.Connection`, `sqlite3.Cursor`, subprocess handle, socket, file object, callable, curses object, or LLM client. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_session_resource_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PERSIST-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Persistence module static audit rejects forbidden side effects. | An AST audit over `brain/ui/persistence.py` confirms imports are confined to the documented seam set (`sqlite3`, `pathlib`, `datetime`, `fractions`, `dataclasses`, `typing`, `types`, `brain.io_types`, `brain.tick` for `BrainState` (typed record) and `assert_state_invariants` (typed helper) only, `brain.tlica.builders`, `brain.tlica.profile`, `brain.tlica.msi`, `brain.tlica.ptcns`, `brain.development.text_stream`, `brain.ui.session`, `brain.ui.commands`); the module imports neither `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, nor `curses`; importing or calling the `tick` callable from `brain.tick` is forbidden (`from brain.tick import tick`, `brain.tick.tick(...)`, and any call target named `tick(...)` are rejected); the module contains no `importlib.import_module`, `__import__`, `eval(`, `exec(`, `compile(`, `atexit.register`, `threading`, `asyncio`, or signal handler; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring). | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PERSIST-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | No kernel-numeric `REAL` column in the schema. | The schema declared in `brain/ui/persistence.py` uses `INTEGER` for every kernel-numeric value (`rho_num`, `rho_den`, `msi_threshold.num`, `msi_threshold.den`, `tick_at_event`), `TEXT` for every identifier / enum name / printable text / timestamp, and contains no `REAL` / `NUMERIC` / `FLOAT` / `DOUBLE` column. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_schema.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PERSIST-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | No long-lived `sqlite3.Connection` on `OperatorSession`. | Save and load helpers use `with sqlite3.connect(...) as conn:` and close the connection on the with-block exit; the static audit asserts that `brain/ui/persistence.py` contains no module-level connection, no class field of type `sqlite3.Connection`, and that no function returns a `sqlite3.Connection` to an external caller; no `OperatorSession` field stores an open connection. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_session_resource_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PERSIST-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store) | Cold-start continuity dry run is inspectable. | `docs/campaigns/phase3_9/PHASE3_9_PERSISTENCE_DRY_RUN.md` documents a deterministic scripted session (`/stream hello world`, `/stream-promote <id>`, `/step`, `/save-session`, relaunch with `--load-session`, verify restored `ScalarProfile` / MSI contents / `PtCns` eval_map / `ContentRegistry` texts / `tick_counter` / `stream_history` / `stream_chunk_serial` / `stream_candidates`); the row is OBSERVED and cannot fail the runner. | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | (none) | OBSERVED |
| I-PERSIST-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.9 Persistent Session Store; reclassified to STRUCTURAL at v0.19) | `brain/ui/persistence.py` owns no autosave trigger or background autosave hook; runtime autosave is owned only by `I-AUTOSAVE-*` and `brain/ui/autosave.py`. | Static AST audit over `brain/ui/persistence.py` confirms no `@atexit.register`, no `threading` / `asyncio` / `signal` handler, no module-level `save_session` call, no tick-adjacent post-dispatch `save_session` call site, and no callable hook registered to fire from any dispatch path; the file contains the typed `save_session` helper definition itself but no autosave invocation. Runtime autosave lives exclusively in `brain/ui/autosave.py`, audited by the `I-AUTOSAVE-11` / `I-AUTOSAVE-13` static rows. The narrowed proposition is enforced by the existing `persistence_static_audit.py` AST audit body; the v0.19 catalog patch reclassifies this row from NOT-EXERCISED to STRUCTURAL with the registration added in `brain/invariants.py` (the fixture file is unchanged). | `brain/ui/persistence.py` | `persistence_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening invariants

These rows are Phase 3.10a engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit, read-mostly operational-hardening layer at `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` over the Phase 3.9 SQLite session store. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize multi-profile / multi-user persistence, network-backed persistence, migrations between schema versions in v1, persistence of LLM client / cache / runtime mode, persistence of operator transcripts beyond bounded session-local state, persistence of curses configuration / terminal state, raw-text-to-`COGITO_ID` mappings, raw-text-to-`BrainState` direct writes, changes to `tick()` semantics, new typed operator commands outside `/session-status` / `/db-status` / `/db-verify` / `/db-backup`, save / export paths outside the configured session DB and the explicit `/db-backup` destination, autosave from any dispatch path (the Phase 3.10c autosave track is gated behind its own review gate and not included in this patch), or any TLICA runtime mutation. `/session-status` reports from in-memory `OperatorSession` fields only and performs no disk IO. `/db-status` opens the configured session DB through `sqlite3.connect("file:<path>?mode=ro", uri=True)` inside a `with conn:` block, reads `meta` rows, and closes. `/db-verify` reuses `load_session` (the Phase 3.9 helper), runs the existing invariant assertions on the candidate `BrainState`, immediately drops the candidate (the live `OperatorSession` reference is unchanged), and returns a typed `DbVerifyReport` with `passed=True` on success and a bounded `error_text` on failure. `/db-backup` uses `sqlite3.Connection.backup()` (page-faithful) from a `mode=ro` source connection to a write-mode destination connection inside `with` blocks; it refuses to overwrite an existing destination unless `force=True`, refuses URI-scheme destinations (`sqlite:`, `file:`, `http:`, `https:`, `ftp:`, `ws:`, `wss:`, `data:`, `gopher:`, `ssh:`, `git:`), and refuses `dest_path == source_path`. The four typed verbs route through `OperatorSession.dispatch` with new `OperatorCommand` kinds (`SESSION_STATUS`, `DB_STATUS`, `DB_VERIFY`, `DB_BACKUP`); none of them calls `tick()` or opens curses; none of them stores a `sqlite3.Connection` on `OperatorSession`. The new CLI short-circuit flags `--db-status` / `--db-verify` / `--db-backup PATH` / `--db-backup-force` are mutually exclusive at argparse time and short-circuit after `--check-terminal` / `--print-once` but before `parse_llm_runtime_args` and curses initialization; they exit with code 0 on success and code 1 on failure; bounded reports go to stdout. `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` imports only the documented seam set (stdlib `sqlite3`, `dataclasses`, `datetime`, `fractions`, `pathlib`, `typing` + `brain.io_types`, `brain.tlica.profile` `COGITO_ID` only, `brain.ui.persistence`, `brain.ui.session`); it does not import `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica` internals beyond what `brain.ui.persistence` re-exports, or `brain.llm`; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring); no `@atexit` / signal / threading / asyncio autosave hook is registered; no autosave entry point exists.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-OPSHARDEN-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/session-status` is read-only and bounded. | `session_status(session)` reads `OperatorSession` fields only with no disk IO, no `tick()`, no curses, and no `sqlite3.Connection`; the returned `SessionStatusReport`'s string fields are bounded by `OPS_REPORT_TEXT_MAX_LEN = 256` and its integer fields are non-negative; `_dispatch_session_status` surfaces the report through `status_message` and leaves the live session field-for-field equal. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_session_status.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-status` is read-only `mode=ro` and bounded. | `db_status(config)` opens the configured DB through `sqlite3.connect("file:<path>?mode=ro", uri=True)` inside a `with conn:` block, reads `meta` rows, closes the connection, and returns a `DbStatusReport`; on a missing DB the report has `db_exists=False`, empty `schema_version` / `catalog_version` / timestamp fields, and a bounded `error_text`; no sqlite3 error propagates and no destination file is touched. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_status.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-verify` reuses `load_session` and DROPS the candidate. | `db_verify(config)` calls `load_session(config)` on the configured DB, captures the `(candidate, LoadSessionResult)` pair, relies on `load_session`'s in-pipeline `assert_state_invariants` over the candidate's `BrainState`, immediately drops the candidate, and returns a `DbVerifyReport` with `passed=True` on success; the live `OperatorSession` reference (`id(session)`) is unchanged before and after the call. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_verify.py`, `persistence_ops_db_verify_drop.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-verify` failure preserves the live session. | A DB with a tampered row (`rho_den=0`, negative `schema_version`, missing meta row, broken FK, malformed `Fraction` pair, etc.) causes `db_verify(config)` to catch the `PersistenceError` and return a `DbVerifyReport` with `passed=False` and a bounded `error_text`; the live `OperatorSession` field-for-field equals the pre-call session; the on-disk DB file byte-equals the pre-call file (`mode=ro` guarantees this). | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_verify.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-backup` uses `sqlite3.Connection.backup()` (page-faithful). | `db_backup(config, dest_path, *, force=False)` opens the source DB in `mode=ro` and the destination DB through `sqlite3.connect(dest_path)` (write mode) inside `with` blocks, calls `source.backup(dest)`, and returns a `DbBackupReport` with non-negative `pages_copied` / `total_pages` / `dest_byte_size`; `load_session` against the destination yields the same `PersistentSessionSnapshot` as the source; `shutil.copyfile` / `shutil.copy2` / `shutil.copytree` are NOT used and the static audit (I-OPSHARDEN-12) rejects them. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_backup.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-backup` refuses to overwrite without `--force`. | When `dest_path.exists()` and `force=False`, `db_backup(config, dest_path, force=False)` returns a `DbBackupReport` with `succeeded=False`, `overwritten=False`, and a bounded `error_text`; no destination write occurs; the same rejection applies to the `/db-backup <path>` composer verb when no `--force` token is supplied; with `force=True` the existing destination is overwritten and `overwritten=True` is reported. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_backup_force.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-backup` refuses URI-scheme destinations. | `dest_path` strings whose scheme is in `DB_BACKUP_FORBIDDEN_SCHEMES = frozenset({"sqlite", "file", "http", "https", "ftp", "ws", "wss", "data", "gopher", "ssh", "git"})` are rejected at argument-validation time as `PersistenceError`; the rejection applies to both the CLI flag (`--db-backup PATH`) and the composer verb (`/db-backup <path>`); no `sqlite3` call is made and no destination file is touched. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_backup_dest_uri.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `/db-backup` never modifies the source DB. | The source connection is opened in `sqlite3` uri `mode=ro`; after a successful backup the source DB file byte-equals the pre-call file; `dest_path == source_path` is rejected as `PersistenceError` before any sqlite3 call. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_db_backup.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | CLI short-circuit ordering and mutual exclusion + exit codes. | `brain/ui/__main__.py` parses `--db-status`, `--db-verify`, `--db-backup PATH`, and `--db-backup-force`; the three new short-circuit flags are mutually exclusive at argparse time (combining them raises a local argument error); they short-circuit AFTER `--check-terminal` and `--print-once` but BEFORE `parse_llm_runtime_args` and curses initialization; on success the process exits with code 0 and on failure with code 1; bounded reports go to stdout (stderr is unused). | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_cli_short_circuit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OPSHARDEN-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | Source connection `mode=ro` during backup. | `db_backup` opens the source connection through `sqlite3.connect("file:<source>?mode=ro", uri=True)` inside `with conn:` and the destination connection without `mode=ro`; the static audit confirms the source open string contains `"mode=ro"` and the destination open string does not, and asserts `source_path` is never used as a write target. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OPSHARDEN-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | Phase 3.10a defensive autosave-absent audit. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` contains no autosave entry point, no `@atexit.register`, no `threading.Thread` / `Timer`, no `asyncio` loop, no signal handler, no curses callback, and no call site that invokes `save_session` outside what is needed for `/save-session` (which lives in the Phase 3.9 dispatcher, not in `persistence_ops`); the audit is a static AST + import-set check. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OPSHARDEN-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `persistence_ops` module static audit. | An AST audit over `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` confirms imports are confined to the documented seam set (`sqlite3`, `dataclasses`, `datetime`, `fractions`, `pathlib`, `typing`, `brain.io_types`, `brain.tlica.profile` for `COGITO_ID` only, `brain.ui.persistence`, `brain.ui.session`); the module imports no `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica` internals beyond what `brain.ui.persistence` re-exports, or `brain.llm`; the module contains no `importlib.import_module`, `__import__`, `eval(`, `exec(`, `compile(`, `atexit.register`, `threading`, `asyncio`, or signal handler; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring). | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OPSHARDEN-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | `persistence_ops` session resource audit. | Phase 3.10a adds no new `OperatorSession` field; after `/session-status`, `/db-status`, `/db-verify`, `/db-backup`, the session field shape is identical to the pre-call shape (no `sqlite3.Connection` / `sqlite3.Cursor` / subprocess handle / socket / file object / callable / curses object appears in any session field); the audit treats `session_store_config` as the only Phase 3.9 addition allowed in `_ALLOWED_SESSION_ATTRS`. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_resource_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OPSHARDEN-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10a Operational Hardening) | Exit-code mapping fixture. | `--db-status` exits with code 0 if the report has `error_text == ""` and `db_exists`, and code 1 otherwise; `--db-verify` exits with code 0 if `passed` and code 1 otherwise; `--db-backup` exits with code 0 if `succeeded` and code 1 otherwise; the mapping is captured in a small dispatcher in `brain/ui/__main__.py` and exercised by the fixture. | `brain/ui/persistence_ops.py` | `persistence_ops_cli_short_circuit.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability invariants

These rows are Phase 3.10b engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit, read-only persistence-observability layer at `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` over the Phase 3.9 SQLite session store. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize multi-profile / multi-user observability, network-backed observability, migrations between schema versions in v1, persistence of LLM client / cache / runtime mode, persistence of operator transcripts beyond bounded session-local state, persistence of curses configuration / terminal state, raw-text-to-`COGITO_ID` mappings, raw-text-to-`BrainState` direct writes, changes to `tick()` semantics, new typed operator commands outside `/db-summary` / `/profile-summary` / `/stream-db-summary` / `/db-diff`, save / export paths outside the configured session DB and the explicit `/db-backup` destination (which is owned by Phase 3.10a), autosave from any dispatch path (Phase 3.10c is deferred), or any TLICA runtime mutation. Every Phase 3.10b helper opens the DB through `sqlite3.connect("file:<path>?mode=ro", uri=True)` inside a `with conn:` block; none of them invokes any kernel builder (`make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns`, `ContentRegistry`, `BrainState`, `make_text_stream_chunk`, `TextStreamHistory`, `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, `OperatorSession`); none of them mutates the live `BrainState` / `OperatorSession`. All `Fraction` values display as exact `"num/den"` strings via a single shared render helper; no `float()`, `repr()`, or JSON leakage appears. `db_diff` reuses the public `snapshot_session` helper promoted from `brain/ui/persistence.py` (the narrow Phase 3.10b extension authorized by the corrigenda) to project the live session and `_deserialize_from_db` to read the saved snapshot; the diff is over the finite field enumeration declared in source (`"profile.<content_id>"`, `"msi.contents"`, `"msi.threshold"`, `"ptcns_eval.<content_id>"`, `"registry.<content_id>"`, `"tick_counter"`, `"stream_chunk_serial"`, `"stream_history.count"`, `"stream_candidates.count"`) and uses the literal `"<missing>"` for one-sided absence (never a silent `0` or `null`). The four typed verbs route through `OperatorSession.dispatch` with new `OperatorCommand` kinds (`DB_SUMMARY`, `PROFILE_SUMMARY`, `STREAM_DB_SUMMARY`, `DB_DIFF`); none of them calls `tick()` or opens curses; none of them stores a `sqlite3.Connection` on `OperatorSession`. `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` imports only the documented seam set (stdlib `sqlite3`, `dataclasses`, `fractions`, `pathlib`, `typing` + `brain.io_types`, `brain.tlica.profile` `COGITO_ID` only, `brain.ui.persistence` for typed records and the promoted `snapshot_session` helper, `brain.ui.session`); it does not import `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica` internals beyond what `brain.ui.persistence` re-exports, or `brain.llm`; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring); no `@atexit` / signal / threading / asyncio autosave hook is registered; no autosave entry point exists.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-OBSERVE-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `/db-summary` reads in `mode=ro`; closed `with` block; bounded report. | `db_summary(config)` opens the DB in `mode=ro` inside `with conn:`, reads `meta` rows plus per-table row counts (`profile_values`, `msi_contents`, `msi_threshold`, `ptcns_eval`, `content_registry`, `stream_chunks`, `stream_candidates`), and returns a `DbSummaryReport` with bounded string fields (`OPS_REPORT_TEXT_MAX_LEN = 256`), non-negative integer fields, and the `msi_threshold` field rendered as the exact `"num/den"` string. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_db_summary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OBSERVE-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `/profile-summary` returns exact-`Fraction` `"num/den"` rows, COGITO first, deterministic sort. | `profile_summary(config, *, row_cap=PROFILE_SUMMARY_ROW_CAP)` reads `profile_values` in `mode=ro`, builds a `tuple[ProfileSummaryRow, ...]` sorted with `COGITO_ID` first then `content_id` ASCII-ascending, renders each `Fraction(num, den)` as the exact `"num/den"` string (`PROFILE_VALUE_STRING_MAX_LEN = 64`), and truncates at `row_cap` with `truncated=True` when the cap is hit; no `float()` / `repr()` / `str(Fraction(...))` leakage; the fixture asserts the render helper is a single named function reused across reports. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_profile_summary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OBSERVE-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `/stream-db-summary` returns bounded head + tail. | `stream_db_summary(config, *, head_cap=STREAM_DB_SUMMARY_HEAD_CAP, tail_cap=STREAM_DB_SUMMARY_TAIL_CAP)` reads `stream_chunks` and `stream_candidates` row counts plus a head slice (first `head_cap` chunks by ordinal) and a tail slice (last `tail_cap` chunks by ordinal); each `StreamDbSummaryRow.text_preview` is bounded by `STREAM_TEXT_PREVIEW_MAX_LEN = 64`; full chunk text is never returned; `truncated=True` iff the chunk count exceeds `head_cap + tail_cap`. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_stream_db_summary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OBSERVE-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `/db-diff` reports finite field enumeration; `"<missing>"` on one-sided absence. | `db_diff(session, config, *, row_cap=DB_DIFF_ROW_CAP)` snapshots the live session via the promoted public `snapshot_session(session)` helper, reads the saved `PersistentSessionSnapshot` in `mode=ro`, and diffs over the finite field enumeration declared in source (`"profile.<content_id>"`, `"msi.contents"`, `"msi.threshold"`, `"ptcns_eval.<content_id>"`, `"registry.<content_id>"`, `"tick_counter"`, `"stream_chunk_serial"`, `"stream_history.count"`, `"stream_candidates.count"`); `DbDiffField.live` / `.saved` use exact `"num/den"` strings for kernel-numeric values, integer text for counters, and the literal `"<missing>"` for one-sided absence; the diff never invents defaults; `truncated=True` iff `diff_count > row_cap`. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_db_diff.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OBSERVE-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | Observability commands never activate saved state and never mutate live `BrainState`. | None of `db_summary` / `profile_summary` / `stream_db_summary` / `db_diff` invokes any kernel builder (`make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns`, `ContentRegistry`, `BrainState`, `make_text_stream_chunk`, `TextStreamHistory`, `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, `OperatorSession`); none mutates `session.state` / `session.stream_history` / `session.stream_candidates` / `session.tick_counter` / `session.stream_chunk_serial`; `session.__eq__` before and after each command is `True`. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_db_summary.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-OBSERVE-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `persistence_observe` module static audit. | An AST audit over `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` confirms imports are confined to the documented seam set (`sqlite3`, `dataclasses`, `fractions`, `pathlib`, `typing`, `brain.io_types`, `brain.tlica.profile` for `COGITO_ID` only, `brain.ui.persistence`, `brain.ui.session`); the module imports no `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica` internals beyond what `brain.ui.persistence` re-exports, or `brain.llm`; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring). | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_static_audit.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-OBSERVE-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10b Persistence Observability) | `persistence_observe.py` contains no builder call. | A static AST audit asserts `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` contains no call to `make_profile_with_cogito`, `make_msi`, `make_ptcns`, `make_text_stream_chunk`, or `make_stream_promotion_candidate`, and no instantiation of `ContentRegistry`, `BrainState`, `TextStreamHistory`, or `OperatorSession`; this complements I-OBSERVE-05 (behavioral non-mutation) with structural absence-of-construction. | `brain/ui/persistence_observe.py` | `persistence_observe_no_builder_call.py` | STRUCTURAL |

### Phase 3.10c Autosave Policy invariants

These rows are Phase 3.10c engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for an explicit, default-off, opt-in autosave layer at `brain/ui/autosave.py` over the existing Phase 3.9 `save_session` helper. They are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize multi-mode autosave (only one non-off mode lands in v1), background autosave / timer / scheduler, autosave on `/quit`, autosave to a journal / rolling backup / network destination / multiple destinations, autosave-driven backup retention, per-tick autosave including failed ticks, migrations between schema versions in v1, persistence of LLM client / cache / runtime mode, a second `save_session` helper, changes to `tick()` semantics, changes to `/step` / `/stream` / `/stream-promote` dispatch bodies beyond returning the outcome boolean, changes to the closed parser verb set beyond the three `/autosave-*` verbs, ambient-environment reads (no `BRAIN_AUTOSAVE_MODE`), a `sqlite3.Connection` on `OperatorSession`, or any TLICA runtime mutation. `AutosaveMode` is a finite closed `(str, Enum)` with exactly `OFF` and `AFTER_SUCCESSFUL_MUTATION`; `AutosaveTrigger` is a finite closed `(str, Enum)` with exactly `STEP_TICK` and `STREAM_PROMOTE`. The default is `OFF` on every cold start at session construction AND at CLI parse time. `/autosave-enable` requires a configured session DB. `maybe_autosave_after_mutation` is the SOLE autosave entry point reachable from any dispatch path, fires AFTER `OperatorSession.dispatch` returns from a successful mutating dispatch (`/step` with `STEP_TICK`, `/stream-promote` with `STREAM_PROMOTE`), never fires after a failed dispatch, never fires after a read-only dispatch, and never fires inside `tick()`. Autosave reuses the Phase 3.9 `save_session` helper via the existing transactional `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` / `COMMIT` / `ROLLBACK` discipline; there is no second save code path. `maybe_autosave_after_mutation` absorbs every `PersistenceError` into the typed `AutosaveStatusReport` (it NEVER raises). Failure preserves the live `OperatorSession` and the on-disk session DB. The persistence module is bounded: `brain/ui/autosave.py` imports only the documented seam set (`dataclasses`, `datetime`, `enum`, `pathlib`, `typing` + `brain.io_types`, `brain.ui.commands`, `brain.ui.persistence`, `brain.ui.persistence_ops`, `brain.ui.session`); it does not import `pickle`, `shelve`, `marshal`, `dill`, `cloudpickle`, `joblib`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.tlica` internals, or `brain.llm`; it contains no `importlib.import_module`, `__import__`, `eval(`, `exec(`, `compile(`, `atexit.register`, `threading`, `asyncio`, or signal handler; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, and class defs (plus a module docstring). `OperatorSession` carries two new optional fields (`autosave_config`, `last_autosave_status`); `_ALLOWED_SESSION_ATTRS` is extended with both names; neither field carries a `sqlite3.Connection`, `sqlite3.Cursor`, callable, socket, subprocess handle, file object, curses object, or LLM client. The outcome-detection contract pins `_dispatch_step_tick` and `_dispatch_stream_promote` to return `Optional[bool]`. A Phase 3.10c autosave dry run is OBSERVED.

| I-AUTOSAVE-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10c Autosave Policy) | Autosave default is `OFF` on every cold start. | `build_default_session()` returns a session whose `autosave_config` is `None` OR whose `autosave_config.mode` is `AutosaveMode.OFF`; argparse default for `--autosave-mode` is the string `"off"`; neither path reads an ambient environment variable (no `BRAIN_AUTOSAVE_MODE` or similar); the two independent default checks (session construction + CLI parse) are consolidated into a single fixture. | `brain/ui/autosave.py` | `autosave_default_off.py` | REQUIRED |

| I-AUTOSAVE-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10c Autosave Policy) | `/autosave-status` returns a bounded report; never raises. | `autosave_status(session)` on a session with any `autosave_config` state returns an `AutosaveStatusReport` with bounded string fields (`OPS_REPORT_TEXT_MAX_LEN=256`), non-negative integer fields, `last_attempt_outcome` in `{"", "ok", "error"}`, and `last_attempt_trigger` in `{"", "step_tick", "stream_promote"}`; the helper never raises. | `brain/ui/autosave.py` | `autosave_status_after_event.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-AUTOSAVE-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.10c Autosave Policy) | `maybe_autosave_after_mutation` never raises. | Calling `maybe_autosave_after_mutation(session, triggered_by=AutosaveTrigger.STEP_TICK)` on a session with any `autosave_config` state returns either `None` or an `AutosaveStatusReport`; on `PersistenceError` from the underlying `save_session` call, the helper absorbs the exception and the returned report carries `last_attempt_outcome="error"` with bounded `last_error_text`; no exception propagates into the dispatcher or curses wrapper. | `brain/ui/autosave.py` | `autosave_failure_preserves.py` | REQUIRED |

This row is the positive complement to the reclassified `I-PERSIST-16` structural row: `I-PERSIST-16` asserts `brain/ui/persistence.py` owns no autosave hook, while `I-AUTOSAVE-11` asserts `brain/ui/autosave.py` is the sole owner that routes through the existing `save_session` helper. | `brain/ui/autosave.py` | `autosave_single_save_path.py` | REQUIRED |

### Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.12c engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded session-local developmental ledger of recurring structural patterns observed in stream/developmental histories at `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py`. The ledger sits strictly *below* truth, agency, `PtCns`, `MSI`, and semantic interpretation, and strictly *above* `TextStreamChunk` / `TextStreamHistory` / `StreamPromotionCandidate`. It is a summary substrate, not a runtime control surface. These rows are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, social/language harnesses, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls (the explicit Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle owns the model-backed seam), real host execution, persistence schema changes (v1 is session-local only: no `pattern_ledger` table, no `SCHEMA_VERSION_V*` bump, no `/save-session` serialization, no `/load-session` restore, no autosave extension), `/pattern-ledger` UI surfaces (DEFERRED in v1 per the accepted Step 9 Option A plan), `/stream-promote` or `/step` observe calls, observe calls on read-only commands or parse / dispatch failures, an aggregate consciousness / sentience / awareness / "I-ness" score, semantic truth / agency / `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` / readability / language / meaning fields, automatic promotion, raw-text-to-`COGITO_ID` mappings, raw-text-to-`BrainState` direct writes, changes to `tick()` semantics or the `_dispatch_step` failure path, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The Pattern Ledger surfaces bounded structural recurrence evidence; it does NOT produce parse trees, language meaning, truth claims, `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` judgments, agency witnesses, aggregate quality scores, consciousness scores, sentience labels, or any subjective claim. Confidence is per-entry only and is the exact `Fraction(recurrence_count, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)` formula.

| ID | Source | Proposition | Python assertion | Owning module | Fixture | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-PLEDGER-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `PatternLedgerSourceKind` is a finite closed enumeration. | `PatternLedgerSourceKind` exposes exactly the documented members (`OPERATOR`, `SYSTEM`, `PROBE_ECHO`, `GENERATED`) whose values mirror `TextStreamSource`; construction with any other value raises `ValueError`. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-02 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `PatternLedgerSaturationState` is a finite closed enumeration. | `PatternLedgerSaturationState` exposes exactly the documented members (`OPEN`, `SATURATED`, `QUIESCED`); construction with any other value raises `ValueError`. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-03 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `PatternLedgerEntry` constructor enforces every bound. | Construction requires a printable bounded `pattern_id` (length at most `PATTERN_LEDGER_ID_MAX` and not equal to `COGITO_ID`), a tuple `signature` with `1 <= len <= STREAM_PATTERN_SIG_MAX` whose every element is bounded printable (length at most `PATTERN_LEDGER_SIGNATURE_ELEM_MAX` and not equal to `COGITO_ID`), tuple-typed `evidence_chunk_ids` and `evidence_candidate_ids` each at most `PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX` with no duplicates and no `COGITO_ID` member, an int `recurrence_count` in `[STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX]`, non-negative `first_seen_tick` and `last_seen_tick` with `last_seen_tick >= first_seen_tick`, a closed `PatternLedgerSourceKind`, an exact `Fraction` `confidence` in `[0, 1]` equal to `Fraction(recurrence_count, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`, a closed `PatternLedgerSaturationState`, and a printable bounded `provenance` (length at most `STREAM_PROVENANCE_MAX_LEN` and not equal to `COGITO_ID`); any violation raises `ValueError` naming I-PLEDGER-03; the resulting record is frozen, exposes no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` / `PCE` / `Act` / `ModeOp` / `AgencyWitness` / `truth` / `readability_score` / `language` / `meaning` / `tick_callback` / `consciousness` / `sentience` / `awareness` field. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-04 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Pattern signatures are structural and non-semantic. | `derive_pattern_signature(chunk)` returns a tuple of bounded printable strings derived only from exact `StreamFeatureVector` values via `extract_stream_features(chunk)`; the signature contains no raw chunk text payload, no `COGITO_ID`, no semantic label, no language label, no readability score, and no truth flag; element count lies in `[1, STREAM_PATTERN_SIG_MAX]`; each element length is at most `PATTERN_LEDGER_SIGNATURE_ELEM_MAX`; repeated derivation on equal inputs returns the same tuple. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_signature_id.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-05 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `pattern_id` is deterministic. | `derive_pattern_id(signature)` returns `"pledger:" + sha256(repr(signature).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()[:16]` for every accepted signature; equal signatures produce equal ids across repeated calls; structurally distinct chunks produce distinct signatures and distinct ids; no nondeterministic source (`time`, `random`, `secrets`, `uuid.uuid4`, `os.getpid`, `socket.gethostname`, `id(...)`, env lookup, hostname) participates in the id path. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_signature_id.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-06 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `recurrence_count` saturates at `STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX`. | A fresh entry created via `PatternLedger().observe(...)` has `recurrence_count = STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MIN`; each subsequent `observe(...)` against the same signature advances the count by exactly 1; the count saturates at `STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX` regardless of how many observations are delivered; direct constructor input outside the range raises (see I-PLEDGER-03). | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-07 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Confidence is exact `Fraction(recurrence_count, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`. | Every observed entry's `confidence` is an exact `fractions.Fraction` in `[0, 1]` computed by `Fraction(recurrence_count, STREAM_PATTERN_RECURRENCE_MAX)`; no `float` / `round` / `math.*` call participates in any module-level function in `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` (defense in depth on the static audit); the entry numeric fields (`recurrence_count`, `first_seen_tick`, `last_seen_tick`) are int with no float drift. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-08 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `PatternLedger` is copy-on-write and bounded. | `PatternLedger.observe(...)` returns a NEW `PatternLedger` and never mutates `self`; the original `entries` tuple identity is preserved; `PatternLedger.entries` is a tuple of `PatternLedgerEntry`, length at most `PATTERN_LEDGER_MAX_ENTRIES`, with no duplicate `pattern_id`; the record is a frozen / slotted dataclass; in-place mutation attempts on `entries` raise. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-09 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | `observe(...)` is idempotent for duplicate evidence delivery. | When the same `chunk_id` (resp. `candidate_id`) is delivered repeatedly against an existing entry, `observe(...)` does NOT append the duplicate to the evidence list, does NOT raise, and does NOT corrupt the existing list ordering; `recurrence_count` may still advance per I-PLEDGER-06; the first `PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX` distinct evidence ids win in arrival order. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-10 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Direct `PatternLedgerEntry` construction with duplicate evidence ids rejects. | Calling `PatternLedgerEntry(...)` with a tuple containing a duplicate `evidence_chunk_ids` or `evidence_candidate_ids` element raises `ValueError` naming I-PLEDGER-03; silent normalization is forbidden at the constructor layer; normalization is the responsibility of `observe(...)` only (see I-PLEDGER-09). | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-11 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Evidence lists cap at `PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX` independently. | `evidence_chunk_ids` length is capped at `PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX = 32` and `evidence_candidate_ids` length is capped independently at the same value; once a list is at cap, further unique ids for that list are no-op appends; the chunk and candidate lists do not share a budget; no FIFO drop, no eviction, no replacement occurs; the earliest `PATTERN_LEDGER_EVIDENCE_MAX` ids are preserved in arrival order. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-12 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | At `PATTERN_LEDGER_MAX_ENTRIES`, a new signature is refused. | When `len(self.entries) == PATTERN_LEDGER_MAX_ENTRIES = 64` and `observe(...)` is called with a previously-unseen signature, the method returns the same `PatternLedger` instance unchanged: no eviction, no LRU, no oldest-drop, no random eviction, no least-confident eviction, no silent overwrite; `observe(...)` against an *existing* signature continues to advance recurrence per I-PLEDGER-06 even at capacity. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_observe.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-13 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Session-local `/stream` integration is the sole v1 observe trigger. | A successful `_dispatch_stream_append` advances `session.pattern_ledger` by exactly one `observe(...)` call (after the chunk and candidate have been appended); the new `pattern_ledger` field is added to `OperatorSession.__slots__` and `_ALLOWED_SESSION_ATTRS`; fresh sessions have `pattern_ledger.entries == ()`; `/stream-summary`, `/stream-candidates`, `/state`, `/tick`, `/session-status`, `/db-summary`, `/profile-summary`, `/stream-db-summary`, `/db-diff`, `/autosave-status`, `/help`, parse-layer rejections, dispatch-layer rejections, `/stream-promote`, `/step` (success and empty-queue failure), `/save-session`, and `/load-session` do NOT call `observe(...)` and leave `session.pattern_ledger` identity-stable; `/step` behavior (tick_counter, queue, state, latest_tick) is bit-for-bit unchanged. | `brain/ui/session.py` | `pattern_ledger_stream_integration.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-14 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Pattern Ledger has no `BrainState` / tick / agency / LLM coupling. | Before and after every `observe(...)` call, `BrainState`, `MSI`, `PtCns`, `ContentRegistry`, `latest_tick`, `tick_counter`, `event_queue`, and source histories are identity-stable; `PatternLedger` and `PatternLedgerEntry` expose no `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` / `PCE` / `Act` / `ModeOp` / `AgencyWitness` / `truth` / `readability_score` / `language` / `meaning` / `tick_callback` / `eval_consistency` / `consciousness` / `sentience` / `awareness` attribute; `brain.development.pattern_ledger` module globals contain neither `tick`, `BrainState`, nor `LLMClient`, and reference no `brain.tick` / `brain.llm.client` / `brain.ui.session` module object. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` + `brain/ui/session.py` | `pattern_ledger_no_runtime_coupling.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-15 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Pattern Ledger module passes the static AST audit. | A static AST audit over `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` rejects every forbidden import (`os`, `subprocess`, `socket`, `urllib`, `http`, `requests`, `pathlib`, `tempfile`, `shutil`, `curses`, `brain.tick`, `brain.llm`, `brain.ui`, every `brain.tlica` submodule other than `brain.tlica.profile`, `threading`, `asyncio`, `atexit`, `signal`, `importlib`, `math`) and every dynamic-execution call (`eval`, `exec`, `compile`, `__import__`, `importlib.import_module`); allowed imports are exactly `dataclasses`, `enum`, `fractions`, `hashlib`, `typing`, `brain.development.text_stream`, `brain.tlica.profile`, and `__future__`; module-level statements are limited to imports, constants, function defs, class defs, and a module docstring; the audit is local to this fixture and does not extend `tools.import_audit`. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_static_audit.py` | REQUIRED |
| I-PLEDGER-16 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Pattern Ledger records carry no unsafe resources. | `PatternLedgerEntry` and `PatternLedger` record fields are bounded primitives, tuples of bounded primitives, `Fraction`, or members of the closed `PatternLedgerSourceKind` / `PatternLedgerSaturationState` enums; no field is a callable, file handle, socket, subprocess handle, `pathlib.Path`, `sqlite3.Connection`, `sqlite3.Cursor`, curses object, or object exposing `eval_consistency`; mirrors the `I-UI-10`-style runtime resource audit. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | `pattern_ledger_no_runtime_coupling.py` | STRUCTURAL |
| I-PLEDGER-17 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Optional `/pattern-ledger` read-only operator command is DEFERRED in v1. | The accepted Step 9 Option A plan defers the `/pattern-ledger` UI to a follow-up reviewed catalog patch. v1 implements only the data substrate and the successful-`/stream`-append observe trigger; no `OperatorCommand.INSPECT_PATTERN_LEDGER` enum member, no `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry for `pattern-ledger`, no `INSPECT_VIEW_MAP` mapping, no parser branch, no dispatcher handler, no view-pane render, and no UI fixture is added. If a future campaign promotes the row to REQUIRED, the dispatch must be read-only: `active_view = "pattern_ledger"` and a bounded printable status line only; no `observe(...)` call, no `tick()` call, and no mutation of `state`, `latest_tick`, `tick_counter`, `event_queue`, `stream_history`, `stream_candidates`, or `stream_chunk_serial`. | `brain/ui/` | (none) | DEFERRED |
| I-PLEDGER-18 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Pattern Ledger) | Pattern Ledger end-to-end scripted walk is NOT-EXERCISED in v1. | No documented Pattern Ledger dry-run helper, OBSERVED summary view, scripted operator walk, audit artifact citation, or external scenario file exists in this campaign; any future end-to-end walk requires an explicit reviewed policy artifact, a dedicated catalog row (promoted from NOT-EXERCISED to OBSERVED), a bounded dry-run helper script, and a stop condition for failure modes; this row exists so a future campaign cannot quietly add an end-to-end Pattern Ledger walk without registering coverage. | `brain/development/pattern_ledger.py` | (none) | NOT-EXERCISED |

### Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor developmental invariants

These rows are Phase 3.12c engineering hypotheses. They bind deterministic Python tests for a bounded read-only structural diagnostic over the existing kernel / session / stream / Pattern Ledger / persistence-config / autosave-config records at `brain/development/coherence_monitor.py`. The Coherence Monitor reads existing records and produces a bounded printable `CoherenceReport`. It performs no I/O, no network, no shell, no subprocess, no filesystem mutation, no sqlite connection, no dynamic execution, no LLM call, no `tick(...)` invocation, no `save_session` / `load_session` / `db_backup` / `db_verify` / `maybe_autosave_after_mutation` call, and no mutation of any kernel container, source history, Pattern Ledger, persistence configuration, or autosave configuration. These rows are not Lean theorem claims and they do not authorize Mode B planning, self-modification, social/language harnesses, natural-language teacher/corrector, real LLM calls (the explicit Phase 3.8b LLM Runtime Toggle owns the model-backed seam), real host execution, persistence schema changes, `/coherence-summary` UI surfaces (DEFERRED in v1 per the accepted Step 13 Option A plan), DB-opening checks from the monitor, an aggregate consciousness / sentience / awareness / "I-ness" score, semantic / truth / agency / `PRESERVE` / `DAMAGE` / readability / language / meaning / belief / intent / self-modification claims in fields or report output, changes to `tick()` semantics or the `_dispatch_step` failure path, or any TLICA runtime mutation. The monitor never claims interior state; report strings use only bounded printable factual phrasing about counts, bounds, and structural agreements among existing records. The Coherence Monitor adds no `OperatorSession` field, no new `OperatorCommand` member, no new `LOCAL_COMMAND_VERBS` entry, no new `ACTIVE_VIEWS` value, no new dispatcher, no new renderer, and no new fixture-allowlist tier in the persistence resource-audit fixtures.

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| I-COHMON-01 | Engineering hypothesis (Phase 3.12c Coherence Monitor) | `CoherenceCheckStatus` is a finite closed enumeration. | `CoherenceCheckStatus` exposes exactly the documented members (`PASS`, `WARN`, `FAIL`, `NOT_APPLICABLE`); construction with any other value raises `ValueError`. The closed `CHECK_SOURCES` set `{"kernel", "session", "stream", "pattern_ledger", "persistence_autosave", "non_claim"}` does not drift. | `brain/development/coherence_monitor.py` | `coherence_monitor_constructor.py` | REQUIRED |
